Cinebench scores are used by system administrators to help make purchase decisions, journalists to review hardware, hardware manufacturers to optimize their latest products, as well as computer owners to evaluate their individual system. \r\n\r\nImprovements to Cinebench Release 20 reflect the overall advancements to CPU and rendering technology in recent years, providing a more accurate measurement of Cinema 4D's ability to take advantage of multiple CPU cores and modern processor features available to the average user.\r\n\r\nCinebench R20 FAQs:\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 uses a much larger and more complex test scene than R15 requiring about 8x the computational power needed to render it. Therefore R15 and R20 results cannot be compared.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 and Cinema 4D R20 incorporate the latest rendering architectures, including integration of Intel’s Embree raytracing technology and advanced features on modern CPUs from AMD and Intel that allow users to render the same scene on the same hardware twice as fast as previously. \r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 provides improved benchmark accuracy for current and next generation CPUs to test if a machine runs stable on a high CPU load, if the cooling solution of a desktop or notebook is sufficient for longer running tasks to deliver the full potential of the CPU, and if a machine is able to handle demanding real-life 3D tasks.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 does not test GPU performance.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 will not launch on unsupported processors. On systems lacking sufficient RAM to load the test scene, a warning will be displayed and the CPU benchmark will not be executed.\r\n\r\n•\tBackground tasks can significantly influence measurement and create diverse results. It's always a good idea to shut down all running programs and disable any virus checking or disk indexing, but it's impossible to eliminate all background processes. Modern operating systems perform various background tasks that cannot or should not be disabled, even though they could have a minor influence on the results.\r\n\r\n•\tTest results can vary slightly because it's impossible to disable every background task of the operating system. These tasks are one factor that may have a slight influence on measurements. Also, modern computers and graphics cards dynamically adjust clock speeds based on environmental conditions like power and temperature. For instance, processors will reduce clock speed when running too hot to allow for cooling and prevent damage. With many modern processors the reverse is also true. They are able to overclock themselves when the temperature is low enough. So, a system freshly started in a relatively cool environment will typically run faster than the same system that has been performing benchmarks for several hours in a heated office.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9P8SWK1JMFB4","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"World National Parks","Images":[{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V2.ImageItem, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ImageType":"tile","Url":"http://store-images.s-microsoft.com/image/apps.8883.14086093697596683.5270012a-5eb9-4710-9ed8-38221303421d.2ba549ab-2680-438d-babf-27831f2309d2","Height":150,"Width":150,"BackgroundColor":"transparent","ForegroundColor":"","Caption":"","ImagePositionInfo":""}],"DisplayPrice":"Бесплатно","Price":0.0,"AverageRating":5.0,"RatingsCount":"3","PackageFamilyNames":["Microsoft.WorldNationalParks_8wekyb3d8bbwe"],"ContentIds":["9fed48b1-769e-7e8b-73fc-c5cd66b57a25"],"GamingOptionsXboxLive":false,"AvailableDevicesDisplayText":"","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"ПК","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"Путешествуйте по всему миру, чтобы посетить впечатляющие национальные парки. При подключении к VPN-серверу, например с помощью Hotspot Shield VPN-прокси, устанавливается защищенное зашифрованное подключение к серверу, находящемуся в другой стране. Так как данные зашифрованы, их нельзя отфильтровать или заблокировать. \r\n\r\n− Зачем использовать VPN\r\nС помощью VPN вы не только сможете разблокировать заблокированные в вашей стране сайты или сервисы, такие как Facebook, Pandora и Youtube; ваша конфиденциальность и безопасность в сети будут значительно выше, поскольку вы просматриваете страницы полностью анонимно (с защитой).\r\n\r\n- Сравнение VPN и прокси\r\nИ VPN, и прокси могут скрыть ваши данные, перенаправляя ваш интернет-трафик и меняя ваш IP-адрес. Однако прокси-сервер полностью основан на браузерных технологиях, и он может быть несовместимым с некоторыми веб-страницами, использующими небраузерные технологии. В отличие от прокси, VPN-сервис шифрует весь ваш трафик и будет работать со всеми интернет-сервисами. В итоге VPN обеспечивает вам большую свободу в сети, а также безопасность и конфиденциальность.\r\n\r\n− Почему Hotspot Shield VPN?\r\nHotspot Shield VPN — это самый надежный в мире VPN с лучшими показателями скорости, стабильности и безопасности.
